from warehouse_details ,Ias_Itm_Wcode

 And i_code = :warehouse_transfer_det.i_code
 And Exists (select 1 from privilege_wh
where u_id=:Parameter.user_no and w_code=warehouse_details.w_code and add_flag=1 and RowNum<=1)
order by warehouse_details.w_code

"PKG INIT"<anonymous>""
SEARCH_ITEM_DTL
Select tr_no   ,
       tr_type ,
       tr_date ,
       tr_ser  ,
       Brn_No  ,
       Ias_Wcode_Pkg.Get_Wc_Nm  (F_W_Code,:Parameter.Lang_No) F_w_code ,
       Ias_Wcode_Pkg.Get_Wc_Nm  ( T_w_code,:Parameter.Lang_No) T_w_code
        From ias_whtrns_mst
         Where ias_whtrns_mst.tr_inout_type = 2
 And   Exists ( Select 1 
                                   From priv_trnsfr_type
                                   Where priv_trnsfr_type.tr_type =ias_whtrns_mst.tr_type
                                    And Nvl(add_flag,1) =1
                                    And  u_id   = :parameter.user_no 
                                    And RowNum <=1 )
 And ((:Parameter.User_No=1) 
        Or Exists (Select 1 From privilege_wh
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No                            
                     And privilege_wh.W_Code = ias_whtrns_mst.W_Code
	             And Nvl(Add_Flag,1) = 1 
	             And Rownum <=1 ))
 And 1 = (Case When :Parameter.User_View_Doc_Entr=0 Then
            1
         Else
           (Select 1 
              From Ias_Shw_Doc_Priv 
             Where U_Id =:Parameter.User_No
               And T_U_Id=Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Ad_U_Id
               And Nvl(Priv_Flag,0)=1
               And Rownum<=1) End)
 And Nvl(tr_post,0) = 0
    And ((:Parameter.User_No=1) 
        Or Exists (Select 1 From S_Brn_Usr_Priv
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No                            
                     And S_Brn_Usr_Priv.Brn_No = ias_whtrns_mst.Brn_No
	             And Nvl(Add_Flag,1) = 1 
	             And Rownum <=1 ))
        Order By Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Tr_Date Desc ,Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Tr_No,Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_Code
Select 
(Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl( :ias_whtrns_dtl.p_size,1)) avlqty 
From item_movement 
 Where I_code      = :ias_whtrns_dtl.I_code 
   And w_code      = Nvl(:ias_whtrns_mst.f_w_code,:ias_whtrns_dtl.f_w_code)
   And expire_date = Nvl(:ias_whtrns_dtl.expiredate,'01/01/1900')
   And batch_no    = Nvl(:ias_whtrns_dtl.batchno,'0')
   Having 
 (Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl( :ias_whtrns_dtl.p_size,1))  > 0
Select     
  Decode( batch_no,'0','', batch_no) batch_no,
(Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl( :ias_whtrns_dtl.p_size,1)) avlqty 
From item_movement
 Where I_code  =:ias_whtrns_dtl.I_code 
   And  w_code = Nvl(:ias_whtrns_mst.f_w_code,:ias_whtrns_dtl.f_w_code)
  And  expire_date= Nvl(:ias_whtrns_dtl.expiredate,'01/01/1900')
  And  batch_no Like  :ias_whtrns_dtl.batchno ||'%'
 Group By batch_no
   Having 
 (Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl(:ias_whtrns_dtl.p_size,1))  > 0
Select  Decode( expire_date ,'01/01/1900','',expire_date) expire_date
  ,Decode(batch_no,'0','', batch_no) batch_no, 
(Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl( :ias_whtrns_dtl.p_size,1)) avlqty 
  From  item_movement 
    Where   I_code = :ias_whtrns_dtl.I_code
    And   w_code =Nvl(:ias_whtrns_mst.f_w_code,:ias_whtrns_dtl.f_w_code)
    And   expire_date like :ias_whtrns_dtl.expiredate ||'%'
  Group By expire_date ,batch_no
Having (Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl( :ias_whtrns_dtl.p_size,1)) >0
Select  w_code ,     
       Decode(expire_date,'01/01/1900','',expire_date) expire_date , 
       Decode(batch_no ,'0','',batch_no) batch_no ,
(Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl( :ias_whtrns_dtl.p_size,1)) avlqty  
 From item_movement
  Where I_code = :ias_whtrns_dtl.I_code 
   And Exists ( Select 1 From Privilege_wh
                      Where Privilege_wh.w_code = item_movement.w_code
                        And add_flag =1 
                        And u_id =:Parameter.user_no 
                        And RowNum <=1 )
 Group By w_code , expire_date ,batch_no
   Having (Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl( :ias_whtrns_dtl.p_size,1)) >0
Select M.I_Code, 
       Decode(:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1,Nvl(M.I_Name,M.I_E_Name),Nvl(M.I_E_Name,M.I_Name)) I_Name,
       D.Itm_Unt,       
       M.I_Desc, 
       M.Vndr_I_Code 
    From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D 
   Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
     And Nvl(D.No_Sale,0) = 0    
     And Get_Items_Activity( M.Activity_No                       ,
                           :Parameter.User_No                 ,
                           :Parameter.Conn_Itm_Act_By_Usr_Priv) = 1  
     And  (:Parameter.User_No = 1  Or Exists (Select 1 From Privilege_Gc
                 Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                   And G_Code = M.G_Code
                   And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1
                   And Rownum <= 1))
     AND M.I_Code Like  Decode(:SEARCH_ITEM_MST.I_Code,Null,'%','%'||:SEARCH_ITEM_MST.I_Code||'%') 
ORDER BY M.I_Code 
Select Manf_Code 
From Ias_Itm_Mst 
Where 
 Manf_Code Like '%'||:Search_Item_Mst.MANF_CODE||'%'
 Order By Manf_Code
Select Group_No,
              Decode(:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1,nvl(Group_A_Name,Group_E_Name), Nvl(Group_E_Name,Group_A_Name)) G_Name 
From IAS_ALTERNATIVE_GROUP
Order By Group_No
Select v_details.v_code,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1, Nvl (v_a_name, v_e_name),
                Nvl (v_e_name, v_a_name)) v_name
  From v_details 
 Where ((:Parameter.User_No = 1)
        Or (((:Parameter.Apalt = 1)
          And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Priv_Acc
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And A_Code = v_details.v_a_code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1 
                      And RowNum <=1 ))
 Or ((:Parameter.Apalt = 2)
            And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Ias_Priv_Vendor
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And v_code = v_details.v_code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1
                      And RowNum <=1 ))))
And  v_code Like      Decode(:Search_Item_Mst.v_code,Null,'%',:Search_Item_Mst.v_code||'%') 
Order By v_code
Select G_Code,   
              Decode(:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1,nvl(G_A_Name,g_E_Name), Nvl(G_E_Name,g_A_Name)) G_Name 
From Group_Details
Where 
:Parameter.User_No = 1
Exists (Select G_Code From Privilege_Gc Where add_Flag=1 And U_Id=:Parameter.User_No And G_Code = Group_Details.G_Code)
 Order By G_Code

From IAS_SUB_GRP_DTL
Where     
:Parameter.User_No = 1
Exists (Select G_Code From Privilege_Gc Where nvl(add_Flag,0)=1 And U_Id=:Parameter.User_No And G_Code = IAS_SUB_GRP_DTL.G_Code and rownum<=1)
 Order By SubG_Code
G_NAME

From IAS_MainSub_GRP_DTL
Where     
:Parameter.User_No = 1
Exists (Select G_Code From Privilege_Gc Where nvl(add_Flag,0)=1 And U_Id=:Parameter.User_No And G_Code = IAS_MainSub_GRP_DTL.G_Code and rownum<=1)
 Order By MnG_Code

null group_name
from cost_centers
where c_s_m=(select cc_type from cost_center_types where affected_by_trans=1) 
and ((:Parameter.User_No=1) OR Exists (select 1 from privilege_cc 
where u_id=:Parameter.User_No and cc_code=cost_centers.cc_code and nvl(add_flag,1)=1 and RowNum<=1  )) 
Order By Decode(:Parameter.P_ord_Lov,1,cc_code,
Decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,cc_a_name,cc_e_name))

RG_TR
SELECT   distinct ias_whtrns_mst.tr_no, ias_whtrns_mst.tr_type, ias_whtrns_mst.tr_ser, ias_whtrns_mst.tr_date, ias_whtrns_mst.w_code, ias_whtrns_mst.tr_desc ,ias_whtrns_mst.Brn_No,ias_whtrns_dtl.Doc_No_Ref
    FROM ias_whtrns_mst,ias_whtrns_dtl
   WHERE ias_whtrns_mst.tr_ser = ias_whtrns_dtl.tr_ser 
     And ias_whtrns_mst.tr_inout_type = 1
     And Nvl(ias_whtrns_mst.Hung,0) = 0
     AND NVL (ias_whtrns_mst.processed, 0) = 1
     And Not Exists (
           select 1 from Ias_Whtrns_dtl dtl
           where Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.doc_ser_ref=dtl.Tr_ser
           And tr_inout_type=2
           And rownum<=1
                         ) 
     AND NVL (ias_whtrns_mst.Stk_Processed, 0) = 0
And ((:Parameter.User_No=1) Or Exists(Select 1 From Priv_Trnsfr_Type Prv
            Where U_Id=:Parameter.User_No 
              And Nvl(Fill_Flag,0)=1 
              And Prv.Tr_Type= Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Tr_Type
              And Rownum<=1))
AND EXISTS
                 (SELECT 1
                    FROM ias_whtrns_dtl Dtl
                   WHERE     Dtl.Tr_Ser = Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Tr_Ser
                         Having Sum(NVL (Dtl.I_Qty, 0) ) >
                             (SELECT SUM (NVL (I_Qty, 0))
                                FROM ias_whtrns_dtl Rcvd
                               WHERE  Rcvd.tr_inout_type = 2 
                                  And Rcvd.F_tr_Ser = Dtl.Tr_Ser
                                Group by Rcvd.F_tr_Ser
                             )
                 group by dtl.Tr_Ser
                 )
And Decode(Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Rtn_Tr,0),0,Nvl(ias_whtrns_mst.t_w_code,0),Nvl(ias_whtrns_mst.F_W_Code,0))=
Decode(Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Rtn_Tr,0),1,:ias_whtrns_mst.w_code,Decode(Nvl(:Parameter.allow_mod_rec_wcode,0),0,:ias_whtrns_mst.w_code,Nvl(ias_whtrns_mst.t_w_code,0)))
ORDER BY ias_whtrns_mst.tr_no, ias_whtrns_mst.tr_type
SELECT   distinct ias_whtrns_mst.tr_no, ias_whtrns_mst.tr_type, ias_whtrns_mst.tr_ser, ias_whtrns_mst.tr_date, ias_whtrns_mst.w_code, ias_whtrns_mst.tr_desc ,ias_whtrns_mst.Brn_No,ias_whtrns_dtl.Doc_No_Ref
    FROM ias_whtrns_mst,ias_whtrns_dtl
   WHERE ias_whtrns_mst.tr_ser = ias_whtrns_dtl.tr_ser 
     And ias_whtrns_mst.tr_inout_type = 1
     And Nvl(ias_whtrns_mst.Hung,0) = 0
     AND NVL (ias_whtrns_mst.processed, 0) = 1
     And Not Exists (
           select 1 from Ias_Whtrns_dtl dtl
           where Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.doc_ser_ref=dtl.Tr_ser
           And tr_inout_type=2
           And rownum<=1
                         ) 
     AND NVL (ias_whtrns_mst.Stk_Processed, 0) = 0
And ((:Parameter.User_No=1) Or Exists(Select 1 From Priv_Trnsfr_Type Prv
            Where U_Id=:Parameter.User_No 
              And Nvl(Fill_Flag,0)=1 
              And Prv.Tr_Type= Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Tr_Type
              And Rownum<=1))
And ias_whtrns_dtl.I_Qty > ( Select Sum(I_Qty) From ias_whtrns_dtl D  
                            WHERE D.tr_inout_type = 2 
                              And D.F_tr_Ser = ias_whtrns_dtl.Tr_Ser
                              And D.Doc_Sequence_Tr = ias_whtrns_dtl.Doc_Sequence_Tr
                           )
And Decode(Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Rtn_Tr,0),0,Nvl(ias_whtrns_mst.t_w_code,0),Nvl(ias_whtrns_mst.F_W_Code,0))=
Decode(Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Rtn_Tr,0),1,:ias_whtrns_mst.w_code,Decode(Nvl(:Parameter.allow_mod_rec_wcode,0),0,:ias_whtrns_mst.w_code,Nvl(ias_whtrns_mst.t_w_code,0)))
ORDER BY ias_whtrns_mst.tr_no, ias_whtrns_mst.tr_type

RG_TR_REC
Select Distinct ias_whtrns_mst.tr_no   ,
ias_whtrns_mst.tr_type ,  
ias_whtrns_mst.tr_ser  , 
ias_whtrns_mst.tr_date ,
ias_whtrns_mst.w_code  ,
IAS_Wcode_Pkg.Get_Wc_Nm(Ias_Whtrns_Mst.w_code ,1) W_Name ,
ias_whtrns_mst.tr_desc ,
ias_whtrns_mst.Brn_No  ,
Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.Doc_No_Ref
From  ias_whtrns_mst,Ias_Whtrns_Dtl
Where ias_whtrns_mst.Tr_Ser = Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.Tr_Ser 
And ias_whtrns_mst.tr_inout_type     = 1 
And Nvl(ias_whtrns_mst.Hung,0)       = 0
And Nvl(ias_whtrns_mst.processed,0)  <> 1
And ((:Parameter.User_No=1) Or Exists(Select 1 From Priv_Trnsfr_Type Prv
            Where U_Id=:Parameter.User_No 
              And Nvl(Fill_Flag,0)=1 
              And Prv.Tr_Type= Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Tr_Type
              And Rownum<=1))
And Not Exists (
select 1 from Ias_Whtrns_dtl dtl
where Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.doc_ser_ref=dtl.Tr_ser
And tr_inout_type=2
And rownum<=1
AND NVL (ias_whtrns_mst.Stk_Processed, 0) = 0
And Nvl(ias_whtrns_mst.t_w_code,0) = Decode(Nvl(:Parameter.allow_mod_rec_wcode,0) ,0,
Decode(Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Rtn_Tr,0),0,:ias_whtrns_mst.w_code,Nvl(ias_whtrns_mst.t_w_code,0)),
Nvl(ias_whtrns_mst.t_w_code,0))
And Decode(Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Rtn_Tr,0),0,Nvl(ias_whtrns_mst.t_w_code,0),Nvl(ias_whtrns_mst.F_W_Code,0))=
Decode(Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Rtn_Tr,0),1,:ias_whtrns_mst.w_code,Decode(Nvl(:Parameter.allow_mod_rec_wcode,0),0,:ias_whtrns_mst.w_code,Nvl(ias_whtrns_mst.t_w_code,0)))
Order By ias_whtrns_mst.tr_no,ias_whtrns_mst.tr_type

RG_A_CODE
select a_code,decode(:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1,A_Name,Nvl(A_Name_Eng,A_Name)) A_name,
decode(:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1,Group_Name,Group_E_Name) Group_Name
 from account,account_grouping 
Where
account.a_grouping=account_grouping.group_no(+)
and Exists  ( Select Account_Type  From Account_Types  Where Nvl (Affected_By_Trans, 0) = 1
And Account_Type = account.A_S_M ) 
and Exists (select 1 from priv_acc where u_id=:Parameter.user_no and a_code=account.a_code and add_flag=1)
order by Decode(:Parameter.P_ord_Lov,1,a_code,
decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,a_name,a_name_eng))

NULL group_name
 from Ias_Projects
where 
  PJ_SUB = 1  
  and ((:Parameter.User_No=1) OR Exists (select 1 from IAS_PRIV_PROJECTS
               where u_id=:Parameter.User_No and Pj_No=Ias_Projects.Pj_No and nvl(add_flag,1)=1 and RowNum<=1  )) 
 Order By Pj_No

  Where 
   Actv_Sub = 1  
  /* And ((:Parameter.User_No=1) OR Exists (Select 1 From Ias_Priv_Actvty
                Where U_Id=:Parameter.User_No 
                 And Actv_No         = Ias_Actvty.Actv_No 
                 And Nvl(Add_Flag,1) = 1 
                 And RowNum <=1  )) */
 Order By Actv_No

RG_C_CODE
Select Customer.C_Code,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1, Nvl (C_A_Name, C_E_Name),
                Nvl (C_E_Name, C_A_Name)) C_Name, 
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1, Nvl (C_Group_A_Name, C_Group_E_Name),
                Nvl (C_Group_E_Name, C_Group_A_Name)) C_Group_Name,
       NULL C_Class_Name
  From Customer,Customer_Group
 Where 
     Customer.C_Group_Code = Customer_Group.C_Group_Code(+) 
 And ((:Parameter.User_No = 1)
        Or (((:Parameter.Aralt = 1)
          And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Priv_Acc
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And A_Code = Customer.C_A_Code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1 
                      And RowNum <=1 ))
 Or ((:Parameter.Aralt = 2)
            And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Ias_Priv_Customer
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And C_Code = Customer.C_Code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1
                      And RowNum <=1 ))))
Order By Lpad(C_Code,30,'0')
C_CODE

RG_I_CODE
Select M.I_Code, Nvl(M.I_Name,M.I_E_Name) I_Name,M.I_E_Name I_E_Name,
         D.Itm_Unt,   
       0 Avl_Qty,
0 I_Price,
         M.I_Desc,
         M.Vndr_I_Code
    From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D 
   Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
     And Get_Items_Activity(M.Activity_No, :Parameter.User_No, :Parameter.Conn_Itm_Act_By_Usr_Priv, 1) = 1
     And (:Parameter.User_No=1 Or Exists(
            Select 1
              From Privilege_Gc
             Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
               And G_Code = M.G_Code
               And Nvl(Add_Flag, 0) = 1
               And Rownum <= 1))
     And (   (Nvl(M.Service_Itm, 0) = 1)
          Or Exists(
                Select 1
                  From Ias_Itm_Wcode
                 Where I_Code = M.I_Code
                   And W_Code = Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_Code, W_Code)
                   And Nvl(Avl_Qty, 0) > 0
                   And Rownum <= 1))
          And Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,
                2, Upper(M.I_Code||M.I_Name||M.I_E_Name||M.I_Desc||M.I_F_Desc),
                3,Upper(M.I_Code||M.I_Name),
                M.I_Code) Like
            Decode(:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code,
                   Null, '%',
                   '%'|| Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,2,Replace(:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code,' ','%'),:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code) || '%')
Order By Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,
                2,Upper(I_Code || M.I_Name),
                M.I_Code),D.LVL_UNIT
I_CODE
I_NAME
I_E_NAME
ITM_UNT
AVL_QTY
I_PRICE
I_DESC
VNDR_I_CODE
RG_I_NAME
Select   Decode(:Parameter.Lang_Dflt,1,Nvl(M.I_Name,M.I_E_Name),Nvl(M.I_E_Name,M.I_Name)) I_Name, 
         M.I_Code, 
         D.Itm_Unt, 
         null Avl_Qty,
         null I_Price,
         M.I_Desc,
         M.Vndr_I_Code
    From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D 
   Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
     And Nvl(D.Main_Unit,0)=1
     And Get_Items_Activity(M.Activity_No, :Parameter.User_No, :Parameter.Conn_Itm_Act_By_Usr_Priv, 1) = 1
     And (:Parameter.User_No=1 Or Exists(
            Select 1
              From Privilege_Gc
             Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
               And G_Code = M.G_Code
               And Nvl(Add_Flag, 0) = 1
               And Rownum <= 1))     
     And Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,
                2, Upper(M.I_Name),
                M.I_Code) Like
            Decode(:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code,
                   Null, '%',
                   Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,
                          3, Null,
                          '%') || :Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code || '%')
Order By Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,
                2,Upper(I_Code || M.I_Name),
                M.I_Code)

SELECT   D.ITM_UNT,
         ROUND(DECODE(:PARAMETER.USER_NO,1, 
               GET_ICODE_AVLQTY (M.I_CODE,D.P_SIZE,:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_CODE),
               GET_ICODE_AVLQTY_PRIV (M.I_CODE,D.P_SIZE,:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_CODE,
               :PARAMETER.USER_NO)),:PARAMETER.NO_OF_DECIMAL) AVL_QTY ,
         Lvl_Unit,
         P_Size
    FROM IAS_ITM_MST M,IAS_ITM_DTL D 
   WHERE M.I_Code=D.I_Code
     AND D.I_Code = :Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code

                     And S_Brn_Usr_Priv.Brn_No = Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Brn_No

and cash_at_bank.bank_no=priv_cash.cash_no 
and ias_cash_at_bank_dtl.a_cy=priv_cash.a_cy
and priv_cash.cash_type=2 
and u_id=:Parameter.User_no and nvl(add_flag,0)=1
and cash_at_bank.Conn_Brn_No =:Parameter.Brn_No

RG_EMP
Select customer.c_code,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1, Nvl (c_a_name, c_e_name),
                Nvl (c_e_name, c_a_name)) c_name,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1, Nvl (c_group_a_name, c_group_e_name),
                Nvl (c_group_e_name, c_group_a_name)) group_name,
       customer.c_a_code a_code
  From customer,Customer_Group
 Where 
     customer.c_Group_Code = Customer_Group.c_Group_Code(+) 
 And ((:Parameter.User_No = 1)
        Or (((:Parameter.Aralt = 1)
          And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Priv_Acc
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And A_Code = customer.c_a_code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1 
                      And RowNum <=1 ))
 Or ((:Parameter.Aralt = 2)
            And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Ias_Priv_customer
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And c_code = customer.c_code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1
                      And RowNum <=1 ))))
And customer.c_a_code = :INV_WRHS_TRNSFR_EXPNS.a_code
Order By Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,1,Lpad(c_code,15,'0') ,Decode(:Parameter.lang_no,1,c_a_name,c_e_name))
Select Emp_No,Decode(:Parameter.Lang_Dflt,1,Nvl(Emp_l_Nm,Emp_F_Nm),Nvl(Emp_F_Nm,Emp_L_Nm)) Emp_Nm
From s_Emp M
Where ((:Parameter.User_No = 1)
        Or 1 =   (Case When Ys_Gen_Pkg.Get_Fld_Value ('IAS_PARA_GEN', 'EMP_PRV_TYP') = 0
                                         Then 1
                                      Else (Select 1
                                              From S_Emp_Prv
                                             Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                                               And Empno_Hrchyno =
                                                      Decode (Emp_Prv_Typ,
                                                              1, M.Emp_No,
                                                              2, M.Hrchy_No
                                                             )
                                               And Decode (:Parameter.Scr_Typ,
                                                           4, View_Flag,
                                                           5, View_Flag,
                                                           Add_Flag
                                                          ) = 1
                                               And Rownum <= 1)
                                   End) )
Order By Emp_No
EMP_NO
EMP_NM

 SELECT   distinct ias_whtrns_mst.tr_no, ias_whtrns_mst.tr_type, ias_whtrns_mst.tr_ser, ias_whtrns_mst.tr_date, ias_whtrns_mst.w_code, ias_whtrns_mst.tr_desc ,ias_whtrns_mst.Brn_No,ias_whtrns_dtl.Doc_No_Ref
											     From 
.Ias_Whtrns_Mst@
.Ias_Whtrns_Dtl@
											   WHERE ias_whtrns_mst.tr_ser = ias_whtrns_dtl.tr_ser 
											     And ias_whtrns_mst.tr_inout_type = 1
											     And Nvl(ias_whtrns_mst.Hung,0) = 0
											     AND NVL (ias_whtrns_mst.processed, 0) = 1
											     AND ias_whtrns_mst.f_tr_ser IN (
											               SELECT f_tr_ser
											                 FROM (SELECT   f_tr_ser, SUM (i_qty)
											                           FROM ias_whtrns_dtl
											                          WHERE tr_inout_type = 1
											                       GROUP BY f_tr_ser
											                       MINUS
											                       SELECT   f_tr_ser, SUM (i_qty)
											                           FROM ias_whtrns_dtl
											                          WHERE tr_inout_type = 2
											                       GROUP BY f_tr_ser))
											     AND NVL (ias_whtrns_mst.t_w_code, 0) =
											            DECODE (
											                    0, 
											                    NVL (ias_whtrns_mst.t_w_code, 0)
											                   )
											ORDER BY ias_whtrns_mst.tr_no, ias_whtrns_mst.tr_type
